\doxysubsection{详细描述}
\subsubsection*{template$<$typename Derived$>$\newline
class Eigen\+::\+Sparse\+Matrix\+Base$<$ Derived $>$}
\doxylink{class_base}{Base} class of any sparse matrices or sparse expressions 


\begin{DoxyTemplParams}{模板参数}
{\em Derived} & is the derived type, e.\+g. a sparse matrix type, or an expression, etc.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyTemplParams}
This class can be extended with the help of the plugin mechanism described on the page \doxylink{TopicCustomizing_Plugins}{Extending Matrix\+Base (and other classes)} by defining the preprocessor symbol {\ttfamily EIGEN\+\_\+\+SPARSEMATRIXBASE\+\_\+\+PLUGIN}.

typedef \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_eigen_1_1_num_traits}{Num\+Traits}}$<$\mbox{\hyperlink{class_eigen_1_1_sparse_matrix_base_a477b2830b50a0a04260463d6f8def336}{Scalar}}$>$\mbox{\hyperlink{boostmultiprec_8cpp_ad5abe8020ead32dcab5e3c15d6d7c30e}{\+::\+Real}} \mbox{\hyperlink{class_eigen_1_1_sparse_matrix_base}{Eigen\+::\+Sparse\+Matrix\+Base}}$<$ Derived $>$\mbox{\hyperlink{bench__gemm_8cpp_acb5c3dc237f99cf17167e8a629f01b43}{\+::\+Real\+Scalar}}}

This is the "{}real scalar"{} type; if the {\itshape \doxylink{class_eigen_1_1_sparse_matrix_base_a477b2830b50a0a04260463d6f8def336}{Scalar}} type is already real numbers (e.\+g. int, float or double) then {\itshape \doxylink{class_eigen_1_1_sparse_matrix_base_aaec8ace6efb785c81d442931c3248d88}{Real\+Scalar}} is just the same as {\itshape \doxylink{class_eigen_1_1_sparse_matrix_base_a477b2830b50a0a04260463d6f8def336}{Scalar}}. If {\itshape \doxylink{class_eigen_1_1_sparse_matrix_base_a477b2830b50a0a04260463d6f8def336}{Scalar}} is {\itshape std\+::complex$<$\+T$>$} then \doxylink{class_eigen_1_1_sparse_matrix_base_aaec8ace6efb785c81d442931c3248d88}{Real\+Scalar} is {\itshape T}.

\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{IsVectorAtCompileTime@{IsVectorAtCompileTime}!Eigen::SparseMatrixBase$<$ Derived $>$@{Eigen::SparseMatrixBase$<$ Derived $>$}}\index{Eigen::SparseMatrixBase$<$ Derived $>$@{Eigen::SparseMatrixBase$<$ Derived $>$}!IsVectorAtCompileTime@{IsVectorAtCompileTime}}}\Hypertarget{class_eigen_1_1_sparse_matrix_base_a2479b95cd20d711e1ef5094f394ea9b4a14a3f566ed2a074beddb8aef0223bfdf}\label{class_eigen_1_1_sparse_matrix_base_a2479b95cd20d711e1ef5094f394ea9b4a14a3f566ed2a074beddb8aef0223bfdf} 
Is\+Vector\+At\+Compile\+Time&This is set to true if either the number of rows or the number of columns is known at compile-\/time to be equal to 1. Indeed, in that case, we are dealing with a column-\/vector (if there is only one column) or with a row-\/vector (if there is only one row). \\
\hline

Flags&This stores expression \doxylink{group__flags}{Flags} flags which may or may not be inherited by new expressions constructed from this one. See the \doxylink{group__flags}{list of flags}. \\

\begin{DoxyNote}{注解}
Even though the returned expression has dynamic size, in the case when it is applied to a fixed-\/size matrix, it inherits a fixed maximal size, which means that evaluating it does not cause a dynamic memory allocation.

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{class_eigen_1_1_sparse_matrix_base_a974f0b277f81e1594ff1dbedc92c42a8} 
template$<$typename Derived$>$ \\
template$<$\mbox{\hyperlink{sugar_8h_ae4f82344f573c70aa1066a2394bba345}{int}} NRows, \mbox{\hyperlink{sugar_8h_ae4f82344f573c70aa1066a2394bba345}{int}} NCols$>$ \\
\mbox{\hyperlink{_dense_base_8h_ad7f74cf0d006b06b945187535404355e}{EIGEN\+\_\+\+DOC\+\_\+\+BLOCK\+\_\+\+ADDONS\+\_\+\+NOT\+\_\+\+INNER\+\_\+\+PANEL}} \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_eigen_1_1_sparse_matrix_base_1_1_fixed_block_xpr}{Fixed\+Block\+Xpr}}$<$ NRows, NCols $>$\mbox{\hyperlink{ir__common_8h_a1ac75f8fee198af783521627f1fecfbc}{\+::\+Type}} \mbox{\hyperlink{class_eigen_1_1_sparse_matrix_base}{Eigen\+::\+Sparse\+Matrix\+Base}}$<$ Derived $>$\mbox{\hyperlink{mimalloc_8h_af7f922b73e3acdb4a430b72f1a1334a5}{\+::block}} (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{struct_eigen_1_1_eigen_base_a554f30542cc2316add4b1ea0a492ff02}{Index}}}]{start\+Row}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{struct_eigen_1_1_eigen_base_a554f30542cc2316add4b1ea0a492ff02}{Index}}}]{start\+Col}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{struct_eigen_1_1_eigen_base_a554f30542cc2316add4b1ea0a492ff02}{Index}}}]{block\+Rows}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{struct_eigen_1_1_eigen_base_a554f30542cc2316add4b1ea0a492ff02}{Index}}}]{block\+Cols}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}

\begin{DoxyReturn}{返回}
an expression of a block in \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}this.
\end{DoxyReturn}

\begin{DoxyTemplParams}{模板参数}
{\em NRows} & number of rows in block as specified at compile-\/time \\
\hline
{\em NCols} & number of columns in block as specified at compile-\/time \\
\hline
\end{DoxyTemplParams}

\begin{DoxyParams}{参数}
{\em start\+Row} & the first row in the block \\
\hline
{\em start\+Col} & the first column in the block \\
\hline
{\em block\+Rows} & number of rows in block as specified at run-\/time \\
\hline
{\em block\+Cols} & number of columns in block as specified at run-\/time\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
This function is mainly useful for blocks where the number of rows is specified at compile-\/time and the number of columns is specified at run-\/time, or vice versa. The compile-\/time and run-\/time information should not contradict. In other words, {\itshape block\+Rows} should equal {\itshape NRows} unless {\itshape NRows} is {\itshape Dynamic}, and the same for the number of columns.

\end{DoxyCodeInclude}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{bottomLeftCorner()}{bottomLeftCorner()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [4/6]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{class_eigen_1_1_sparse_matrix_base_abb4347d8e16bd8f4889a65f933526088} 
template$<$typename Derived$>$ \\
template$<$\mbox{\hyperlink{sugar_8h_ae4f82344f573c70aa1066a2394bba345}{int}} CRows, \mbox{\hyperlink{sugar_8h_ae4f82344f573c70aa1066a2394bba345}{int}} CCols$>$ \\
\mbox{\hyperlink{_dense_base_8h_ad7f74cf0d006b06b945187535404355e}{EIGEN\+\_\+\+DOC\+\_\+\+BLOCK\+\_\+\+ADDONS\+\_\+\+NOT\+\_\+\+INNER\+\_\+\+PANEL}} \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_eigen_1_1_sparse_matrix_base_1_1_fixed_block_xpr}{Fixed\+Block\+Xpr}}$<$ CRows, CCols $>$\mbox{\hyperlink{ir__common_8h_a1ac75f8fee198af783521627f1fecfbc}{\+::\+Type}} \mbox{\hyperlink{class_eigen_1_1_sparse_matrix_base}{Eigen\+::\+Sparse\+Matrix\+Base}}$<$ Derived $>$\+::bottom\+Left\+Corner (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{struct_eigen_1_1_eigen_base_a554f30542cc2316add4b1ea0a492ff02}{Index}}}]{c\+Rows}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{struct_eigen_1_1_eigen_base_a554f30542cc2316add4b1ea0a492ff02}{Index}}}]{c\+Cols}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}

\begin{DoxyReturn}{返回}
an expression of a bottom-\/left corner of \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}this.
\end{DoxyReturn}

\begin{DoxyTemplParams}{模板参数}
{\em CRows} & number of rows in corner as specified at compile-\/time \\
\hline
{\em CCols} & number of columns in corner as specified at compile-\/time \\
\hline
\end{DoxyTemplParams}

\begin{DoxyParams}{参数}
{\em c\+Rows} & number of rows in corner as specified at run-\/time \\
\hline
{\em c\+Cols} & number of columns in corner as specified at run-\/time\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
This function is mainly useful for corners where the number of rows is specified at compile-\/time and the number of columns is specified at run-\/time, or vice versa. The compile-\/time and run-\/time information should not contradict. In other words, {\itshape c\+Rows} should equal {\itshape CRows} unless {\itshape CRows} is {\itshape Dynamic}, and the same for the number of columns.

Example\+:

\end{DoxyCodeInclude}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{bottomRightCorner()}{bottomRightCorner()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [4/6]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{class_eigen_1_1_sparse_matrix_base_ae9fe1f2a68c22085a3751ea9b086140c} 
template$<$typename Derived$>$ \\
template$<$\mbox{\hyperlink{sugar_8h_ae4f82344f573c70aa1066a2394bba345}{int}} CRows, \mbox{\hyperlink{sugar_8h_ae4f82344f573c70aa1066a2394bba345}{int}} CCols$>$ \\
\mbox{\hyperlink{_dense_base_8h_ad7f74cf0d006b06b945187535404355e}{EIGEN\+\_\+\+DOC\+\_\+\+BLOCK\+\_\+\+ADDONS\+\_\+\+NOT\+\_\+\+INNER\+\_\+\+PANEL}} \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_eigen_1_1_sparse_matrix_base_1_1_fixed_block_xpr}{Fixed\+Block\+Xpr}}$<$ CRows, CCols $>$\mbox{\hyperlink{ir__common_8h_a1ac75f8fee198af783521627f1fecfbc}{\+::\+Type}} \mbox{\hyperlink{class_eigen_1_1_sparse_matrix_base}{Eigen\+::\+Sparse\+Matrix\+Base}}$<$ Derived $>$\+::bottom\+Right\+Corner (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{struct_eigen_1_1_eigen_base_a554f30542cc2316add4b1ea0a492ff02}{Index}}}]{c\+Rows}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{struct_eigen_1_1_eigen_base_a554f30542cc2316add4b1ea0a492ff02}{Index}}}]{c\+Cols}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}

\begin{DoxyReturn}{返回}
an expression of a bottom-\/right corner of \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}this.
\end{DoxyReturn}

\begin{DoxyTemplParams}{模板参数}
{\em CRows} & number of rows in corner as specified at compile-\/time \\
\hline
{\em CCols} & number of columns in corner as specified at compile-\/time \\
\hline
\end{DoxyTemplParams}

\begin{DoxyParams}{参数}
{\em c\+Rows} & number of rows in corner as specified at run-\/time \\
\hline
{\em c\+Cols} & number of columns in corner as specified at run-\/time\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
This function is mainly useful for corners where the number of rows is specified at compile-\/time and the number of columns is specified at run-\/time, or vice versa. The compile-\/time and run-\/time information should not contradict. In other words, {\itshape c\+Rows} should equal {\itshape CRows} unless {\itshape CRows} is {\itshape Dynamic}, and the same for the number of columns.

\begin{DoxyWarning}{警告}

In order to check for equality between two vectors or matrices with floating-\/point coefficients, it is generally a far better idea to use a fuzzy comparison as provided by \doxylink{class_eigen_1_1_sparse_matrix_base_a70851868f2d1dbf53bcf1fa1e5c1c970}{is\+Approx()} and is\+Much\+Smaller\+Than().

\begin{DoxyWarning}{警告}
this performs an exact comparison, which is generally a bad idea with floating-\/point types. In order to check for equality between two vectors or matrices with floating-\/point coefficients, it is generally a far better idea to use a fuzzy comparison as provided by \doxylink{class_eigen_1_1_sparse_matrix_base_a70851868f2d1dbf53bcf1fa1e5c1c970}{is\+Approx()} and is\+Much\+Smaller\+Than().
\end{DoxyWarning}
Example\+: 
\begin{DoxyCodeInclude}{0}

\end{DoxyCodeInclude}
 Output\+: 
\begin{DoxyVerbInclude}
\end{DoxyVerbInclude}

\end{DoxySeeAlso}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{class_eigen_1_1_sparse_matrix_base_a6b3f24af4a70e2824a52fbe909872274}

EIGEN\+\_\+\+DEVICE\+\_\+\+FUNC \mbox{\hyperlink{class_eigen_1_1_sparse_matrix_base_a47e794920c3c0d339440979acb445c35}{Segment\+Return\+Type}} \mbox{\hyperlink{class_eigen_1_1_sparse_matrix_base}{Eigen\+::\+Sparse\+Matrix\+Base}}$<$ Derived $>$\+::head (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{struct_eigen_1_1_eigen_base_a554f30542cc2316add4b1ea0a492ff02}{Index}}}]{n}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}

\begin{DoxyReturn}{返回}
a dynamic-\/size expression of the first coefficients of \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}this.
\end{DoxyReturn}
\textbackslash{}only\+\_\+for\+\_\+vectors


\begin{DoxyParams}{参数}
{\em n} & the number of coefficients in the segment\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
Example\+: 
\begin{DoxyCodeInclude}{0}

\end{DoxyCodeInclude}
 Output\+: 
\begin{DoxyVerbInclude}
\end{DoxyVerbInclude}


\begin{DoxyNote}{注解}
Even though the returned expression has dynamic size, in the case when it is applied to a fixed-\/size vector, it inherits a fixed maximal size, which means that evaluating it does not cause a dynamic memory allocation.
\end{DoxyNote}

a fixed-\/size expression of the first coefficients of \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}this.

\textbackslash{}only\+\_\+for\+\_\+vectors


\begin{DoxyTemplParams}{模板参数}
{\em N} & the number of coefficients in the segment as specified at compile-\/time \\
\hline
\end{DoxyTemplParams}

\begin{DoxyParams}{参数}
{\em n} & the number of coefficients in the segment as specified at run-\/time\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
The compile-\/time and run-\/time information should not contradict. In other words, {\itshape n} should equal {\itshape N} unless {\itshape N} is {\itshape Dynamic}.

\index{operator\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}@{operator\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}!Eigen::SparseMatrixBase$<$ Derived $>$@{Eigen::SparseMatrixBase$<$ Derived $>$}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{operator\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}()}{operator*()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [3/3]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{class_eigen_1_1_sparse_matrix_base_a9d4d71b3f34389e6fc01f2b86e43f7a4} 
template$<$typename Derived$>$ \\
template$<$typename Other\+Derived$>$ \\
const \mbox{\hyperlink{class_eigen_1_1_product}{Product}}$<$ Derived, Other\+Derived, \mbox{\hyperlink{namespace_eigen_a15a3e26ba06f3c60d2f2e46f56045f27ab4d020163beae2ddb3ca6cdd296136bf}{Alias\+Free\+Product}} $>$ \mbox{\hyperlink{class_eigen_1_1_sparse_matrix_base}{Eigen\+::\+Sparse\+Matrix\+Base}}$<$ Derived $>$\+::operator\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{class_eigen_1_1_sparse_matrix_base}{Sparse\+Matrix\+Base}}$<$ Other\+Derived $>$ \&}]{other}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption}) const\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}

\begin{DoxyReturn}{返回}
an expression of the product of two sparse matrices. By default a conservative product preserving the symbolic non zeros is performed. The automatic pruning of the small values can be achieved by calling the \doxylink{class_eigen_1_1_sparse_matrix_base_ac8d0414b56d9d620ce9a698c1b281e5d}{pruned()} function in which case a totally different product algorithm is employed\+: 
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\mbox{\hyperlink{test__buffer__node_8cpp_ac4cf4b2ab929bd23951a8676eeac086b}{C}}\ =\ (\mbox{\hyperlink{bench__gemm_8cpp_addc86e8508f14411ec98f521c520f875}{A}}*\mbox{\hyperlink{bench__gemm_8cpp_a37a83060ac796961b44991c836f083f7}{B}}).\mbox{\hyperlink{class_eigen_1_1_sparse_matrix_base_ac8d0414b56d9d620ce9a698c1b281e5d}{pruned}}();\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ supress\ numerical\ zeros\ (exact)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\mbox{\hyperlink{test__buffer__node_8cpp_ac4cf4b2ab929bd23951a8676eeac086b}{C}}\ =\ (\mbox{\hyperlink{bench__gemm_8cpp_addc86e8508f14411ec98f521c520f875}{A}}*\mbox{\hyperlink{bench__gemm_8cpp_a37a83060ac796961b44991c836f083f7}{B}}).\mbox{\hyperlink{class_eigen_1_1_sparse_matrix_base_ac8d0414b56d9d620ce9a698c1b281e5d}{pruned}}(ref);}
\DoxyCodeLine{\mbox{\hyperlink{test__buffer__node_8cpp_ac4cf4b2ab929bd23951a8676eeac086b}{C}}\ =\ (\mbox{\hyperlink{bench__gemm_8cpp_addc86e8508f14411ec98f521c520f875}{A}}*\mbox{\hyperlink{bench__gemm_8cpp_a37a83060ac796961b44991c836f083f7}{B}}).\mbox{\hyperlink{class_eigen_1_1_sparse_matrix_base_ac8d0414b56d9d620ce9a698c1b281e5d}{pruned}}(ref,epsilon);}

\end{DoxyCode}
 where {\ttfamily ref} is a meaningful non zero reference value. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

\end{DoxyReturn}
This method is typically used in conjunction with the product of two sparse matrices to automatically prune the smallest values as follows\+:

\DoxyCodeLine{\mbox{\hyperlink{test__buffer__node_8cpp_ac4cf4b2ab929bd23951a8676eeac086b}{C}}\ =\ (\mbox{\hyperlink{bench__gemm_8cpp_addc86e8508f14411ec98f521c520f875}{A}}*\mbox{\hyperlink{bench__gemm_8cpp_a37a83060ac796961b44991c836f083f7}{B}}).\mbox{\hyperlink{class_eigen_1_1_sparse_matrix_base_ac8d0414b56d9d620ce9a698c1b281e5d}{pruned}}(ref);}
\DoxyCodeLine{\mbox{\hyperlink{test__buffer__node_8cpp_ac4cf4b2ab929bd23951a8676eeac086b}{C}}\ =\ (\mbox{\hyperlink{bench__gemm_8cpp_addc86e8508f14411ec98f521c520f875}{A}}*\mbox{\hyperlink{bench__gemm_8cpp_a37a83060ac796961b44991c836f083f7}{B}}).\mbox{\hyperlink{class_eigen_1_1_sparse_matrix_base_ac8d0414b56d9d620ce9a698c1b281e5d}{pruned}}(ref,epsilon);}

\begin{DoxyVerbInclude}
\end{DoxyVerbInclude}


\begin{DoxyNote}{注解}
Even though the returned expression has dynamic size, in the case when it is applied to a fixed-\/size vector, it inherits a fixed maximal size, which means that evaluating it does not cause a dynamic memory allocation.
\end{DoxyNote}

EIGEN\+\_\+\+DEVICE\+\_\+\+FUNC \mbox{\hyperlink{class_eigen_1_1_sparse_matrix_base_a47e794920c3c0d339440979acb445c35}{Segment\+Return\+Type}} \mbox{\hyperlink{class_eigen_1_1_sparse_matrix_base}{Eigen\+::\+Sparse\+Matrix\+Base}}$<$ Derived $>$\+::tail (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{struct_eigen_1_1_eigen_base_a554f30542cc2316add4b1ea0a492ff02}{Index}}}]{n}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}

a dynamic-\/size expression of the last coefficients of \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}this.
\end{DoxyReturn}

\begin{DoxyCodeInclude}{0}

\end{DoxyCodeInclude}
 Output\+: 
\begin{DoxyVerbInclude}
\end{DoxyVerbInclude}


\begin{DoxyNote}{注解}
Even though the returned expression has dynamic size, in the case when it is applied to a fixed-\/size vector, it inherits a fixed maximal size, which means that evaluating it does not cause a dynamic memory allocation.
\end{DoxyNote}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{class_eigen_1_1_sparse_matrix_base_a6a1e2d8f669314555e2efe9eb7434cdd} 
template$<$typename Derived$>$ \\
template$<$\mbox{\hyperlink{sugar_8h_ae4f82344f573c70aa1066a2394bba345}{int}} CRows, \mbox{\hyperlink{sugar_8h_ae4f82344f573c70aa1066a2394bba345}{int}} CCols$>$ \\
\mbox{\hyperlink{_dense_base_8h_ad7f74cf0d006b06b945187535404355e}{EIGEN\+\_\+\+DOC\+\_\+\+BLOCK\+\_\+\+ADDONS\+\_\+\+NOT\+\_\+\+INNER\+\_\+\+PANEL}} \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_eigen_1_1_sparse_matrix_base_1_1_fixed_block_xpr}{Fixed\+Block\+Xpr}}$<$ CRows, CCols $>$\mbox{\hyperlink{ir__common_8h_a1ac75f8fee198af783521627f1fecfbc}{\+::\+Type}} \mbox{\hyperlink{class_eigen_1_1_sparse_matrix_base}{Eigen\+::\+Sparse\+Matrix\+Base}}$<$ Derived $>$\+::top\+Left\+Corner (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{struct_eigen_1_1_eigen_base_a554f30542cc2316add4b1ea0a492ff02}{Index}}}]{c\+Rows}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{struct_eigen_1_1_eigen_base_a554f30542cc2316add4b1ea0a492ff02}{Index}}}]{c\+Cols}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}

\begin{DoxyReturn}{返回}
an expression of a top-\/left corner of \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}this.
\end{DoxyReturn}

\begin{DoxyTemplParams}{模板参数}
{\em CRows} & number of rows in corner as specified at compile-\/time \\
\hline
{\em CCols} & number of columns in corner as specified at compile-\/time \\
\hline
\end{DoxyTemplParams}

\begin{DoxyParams}{参数}
{\em c\+Rows} & number of rows in corner as specified at run-\/time \\
\hline
{\em c\+Cols} & number of columns in corner as specified at run-\/time\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
This function is mainly useful for corners where the number of rows is specified at compile-\/time and the number of columns is specified at run-\/time, or vice versa. The compile-\/time and run-\/time information should not contradict. In other words, {\itshape c\+Rows} should equal {\itshape CRows} unless {\itshape CRows} is {\itshape Dynamic}, and the same for the number of columns.

Example\+:

\end{DoxyCodeInclude}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{topRightCorner()}{topRightCorner()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [4/6]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{class_eigen_1_1_sparse_matrix_base_a550b27ebc7ff9b4657d6a49e15e93399} 
template$<$typename Derived$>$ \\
template$<$\mbox{\hyperlink{sugar_8h_ae4f82344f573c70aa1066a2394bba345}{int}} CRows, \mbox{\hyperlink{sugar_8h_ae4f82344f573c70aa1066a2394bba345}{int}} CCols$>$ \\
\mbox{\hyperlink{_dense_base_8h_ad7f74cf0d006b06b945187535404355e}{EIGEN\+\_\+\+DOC\+\_\+\+BLOCK\+\_\+\+ADDONS\+\_\+\+NOT\+\_\+\+INNER\+\_\+\+PANEL}} \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_eigen_1_1_sparse_matrix_base_1_1_fixed_block_xpr}{Fixed\+Block\+Xpr}}$<$ CRows, CCols $>$\mbox{\hyperlink{ir__common_8h_a1ac75f8fee198af783521627f1fecfbc}{\+::\+Type}} \mbox{\hyperlink{class_eigen_1_1_sparse_matrix_base}{Eigen\+::\+Sparse\+Matrix\+Base}}$<$ Derived $>$\+::top\+Right\+Corner (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{struct_eigen_1_1_eigen_base_a554f30542cc2316add4b1ea0a492ff02}{Index}}}]{c\+Rows}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{struct_eigen_1_1_eigen_base_a554f30542cc2316add4b1ea0a492ff02}{Index}}}]{c\+Cols}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}

\begin{DoxyReturn}{返回}
an expression of a top-\/right corner of \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}this.
\end{DoxyReturn}

\begin{DoxyTemplParams}{模板参数}
{\em CRows} & number of rows in corner as specified at compile-\/time \\
\hline
{\em CCols} & number of columns in corner as specified at compile-\/time \\
\hline
\end{DoxyTemplParams}

\begin{DoxyParams}{参数}
{\em c\+Rows} & number of rows in corner as specified at run-\/time \\
\hline
{\em c\+Cols} & number of columns in corner as specified at run-\/time\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
This function is mainly useful for corners where the number of rows is specified at compile-\/time and the number of columns is specified at run-\/time, or vice versa. The compile-\/time and run-\/time information should not contradict. In other words, {\itshape c\+Rows} should equal {\itshape CRows} unless {\itshape CRows} is {\itshape Dynamic}, and the same for the number of columns.
